	<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" >Support gem</h1>
	<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
		<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Path of Exile Wiki</div>
		<div id="contentSub"></div>
		<div id="contentSub2"></div>
		
		<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">Jump to search</a>
		<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en-GB" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="info-card"><div class="info-card&#95;_card"><div class="info-card&#95;_header"><div class="left"></div><div class="middle"><div class="heading">Support Skill Gems</div><div class="subheading"><a href="/wiki/Item_class" title="Item class">Item class</a><abbr title="Item classes categorize items. Classes are often used to restrict items or skill gems to a specific class or by item filters">(?)</abbr></div></div><div class="right"></div></div><div class="info-card&#95;_body"><div class="block">Also referred to as: <ul><li>support gems</li><li>supports</li></ul></div><div class="block">Item filter ID: Support Skill Gem</div></div></div></div>
<div class="hatnote">
<div class="hatnote&#95;_icon"></div>
<div class="hatnote&#95;_text">For a detailed description of the interaction between active skill gem and support gems, see <a href="/wiki/Gem" title="Gem">gem</a>.</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:154px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Socket.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="/w/images/b/b0/Socket.png" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="152" height="171" class="thumbimage" data-file-width="152" data-file-height="171" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Socket.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>To support an active skill, the support gem has to be placed in a socket linked to the socket of the active gem.</div></div></div>
<p><b>Support Skill Gems</b>, more commonly referred to as <b>support gems</b> or just <b>supports</b> are an <a href="/wiki/Item_class" title="Item class">item class</a> used to augment <a href="/wiki/Active_skill_gems" class="mw-redirect" title="Active skill gems">active skill gems</a> (or known as "skill gem").
</p><p>They are socketed in the same way as <a href="/wiki/Active_skill_gem" class="mw-redirect" title="Active skill gem">active skill gems</a>, with the difference that they do not give access to another active skill. Instead, they modify any active skill gems in sockets linked to the support gem, while also typically increasing the <a href="/wiki/Mana" title="Mana">mana</a> cost of the skill. The modifications vary based on both the active skill being altered and the support gem, and certain skill gem - support gem combinations will leave the skill unmodified. For instance a <span class="c-item-hoverbox"><span class="c-item-hoverbox&#95;_activator"><img alt="" src="/w/images/thumb/0/09/Clarity_inventory_icon.png/16px-Clarity_inventory_icon.png" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="16" height="16" srcset="/w/images/thumb/0/09/Clarity_inventory_icon.png/24px-Clarity_inventory_icon.png 1.5x, /w/images/thumb/0/09/Clarity_inventory_icon.png/32px-Clarity_inventory_icon.png 2x" data-file-width="78" data-file-height="78" /><a href="/wiki/Clarity" title="Clarity">Clarity</a></span><span class="c-item-hoverbox&#95;_display"><span class="item-box -gem"><span class="header -single"><span class="symbol"></span>Clarity<span class="symbol"></span></span><span class="item-stats"><span class="group"><a href="/wiki/Category:Aura_(gem_tag)" title="Category:Aura (gem tag)">Aura</a>, <a href="/wiki/Category:Spell_(gem_tag)" title="Category:Spell (gem tag)">Spell</a>, <a href="/wiki/Category:AoE_(gem_tag)" title="Category:AoE (gem tag)">AoE</a><br />Level: <em class="tc -value">(1-20)</em><br />Reservation: <em class="tc -value">(34-279) Mana</em><br />Cooldown Time: <em class="tc -value">1.20 sec</em><br />Can Store <em class="tc -value">1</em> Use(s)<br />Cast Time: <em class="tc -value">Instant</em><br />Radius: <em class="tc -value">36</em></span><span class="group">Requires Level <em class="tc -value"><em class="tc -value">10</em></em></span><span class="group tc -gemdesc">Casts an aura that grants mana regeneration to you and your allies.</span><span class="group tc -mod"><span class="quality"><span class="quality-header"><span><em class="tc -default">Per 1% Quality:</em></span><span class="quality-section-select quality-1 quality-selected">1<span>Superior</span></span><span class="quality-section-select quality-2">2<span>Anomalous</span></span><span class="quality-section-select quality-3">3<span>Divergent</span></span></span><span class="quality-box quality-1 quality-selected">2% increased Area of Effect</span><span class="quality-box quality-2">You and nearby Allies have 0.25% increased Mana Recovery from Flasks</span><span class="quality-box quality-3">You and nearby Allies have 0.25% increased Damage while on Full Mana</span></span></span><span class="group tc -mod">You and nearby Allies Regenerate (2.9-33) Mana per second<br />+(0-19) to radius</span><span class="group tc -help">Place into an item socket of the right colour to gain this skill. Right click to remove from a socket.</span></span><a href="/wiki/File:Clarity_skill_icon.png" class="image"><img alt="Clarity skill icon.png" src="/w/images/8/8b/Clarity_skill_icon.png" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="64" height="64" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span><img alt="" src="/w/images/0/09/Clarity_inventory_icon.png" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="78" height="78" data-file-width="78" data-file-height="78" /></span></span> gem linked with <span class="c-item-hoverbox"><span class="c-item-hoverbox&#95;_activator"><img alt="" src="/w/images/thumb/5/5b/Added_Fire_Damage_Support_inventory_icon.png/16px-Added_Fire_Damage_Support_inventory_icon.png" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="16" height="16" srcset="/w/images/thumb/5/5b/Added_Fire_Damage_Support_inventory_icon.png/24px-Added_Fire_Damage_Support_inventory_icon.png 1.5x, /w/images/thumb/5/5b/Added_Fire_Damage_Support_inventory_icon.png/32px-Added_Fire_Damage_Support_inventory_icon.png 2x" data-file-width="78" data-file-height="78" /><a href="/wiki/Added_Fire_Damage_Support" title="Added Fire Damage Support">Added Fire Damage Support</a></span><span class="c-item-hoverbox&#95;_display"><span class="item-box -gem"><span class="header -single"><span class="symbol"></span>Added Fire Damage Support<span class="symbol"></span></span><span class="item-stats"><span class="group"><a href="/wiki/Category:Fire_(gem_tag)" title="Category:Fire (gem tag)">Fire</a>, <a href="/wiki/Category:Physical_(gem_tag)" title="Category:Physical (gem tag)">Physical</a>, <a href="/wiki/Category:Support_(gem_tag)" title="Category:Support (gem tag)">Support</a><br />Icon: <em class="tc -value"><span class="support-gem-id-red">F</span></em><br />Level: <em class="tc -value">(1-20)</em><br />Cost &amp; Reservation Multiplier: <em class="tc -value">120%</em></span><span class="group">Requires Level <em class="tc -value"><em class="tc -value">8</em></em></span><span class="group tc -gemdesc">Supports any skill that hits enemies.</span><span class="group tc -mod"><span class="quality"><span class="quality-header"><span><em class="tc -default">Per 1% Quality:</em></span><span class="quality-section-select quality-1 quality-selected">1<span>Superior</span></span><span class="quality-section-select quality-2">2<span>Anomalous</span></span><span class="quality-section-select quality-3">3<span>Divergent</span></span></span><span class="quality-box quality-1 quality-selected">Supported Skills deal 0.5% increased Fire Damage</span><span class="quality-box quality-2">Supported Skills deal 1% reduced Fire Damage<br />Supported Skills have +1% to Fire Damage over Time Multiplier</span><span class="quality-box quality-3">Supported Skills have 1% of Physical Damage Converted to Fire Damage</span></span></span><span class="group tc -mod">Supported Skills gain (25-39)% of Physical Damage as Extra Fire Damage</span><span class="group tc -help">This is a Support Gem. It does not grant a bonus to your character, but to skills in sockets connected to it. Place into an item socket connected to a socket containing the Active Skill Gem you wish to augment. Right click to remove from a socket.</span></span></span><img alt="" src="/w/images/5/5b/Added_Fire_Damage_Support_inventory_icon.png" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="78" height="78" data-file-width="78" data-file-height="78" /></span></span> remains unchanged. Please note that <a href="/wiki/Gem_tag" title="Gem tag">gem tags</a> <b>do not</b> determine the supportability.<sup id="cite_ref-ref1_1-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ref1-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Multiple skill gems may be linked to a support gem, in which case it will modify all of the skills, and multiple support gems may be linked to a skill gem, in which case it will be modified by all of them. However, if two copies of a support gem are linked to the same skill, only the higher level gem will be used. If a <a href="/wiki/Body_armour" title="Body armour">body armour</a> contains two copies of a skill gem linked to different sets of support gems, two separate versions of the skill will be available, each with their own modifications. This may be desirable if for instance one version has been modified for single target damage, while another has been modified for <a href="/wiki/Area_of_effect" title="Area of effect">area of effect</a> damage. Support Gems add an icon in the form of a coloured letter or symbol to any supported skills' icons on the <a href="/wiki/Skill_bar" title="Skill bar">Skill Bar</a>. 
</p><p>In terms of modifiers, support gems with # gem tag  (e.g. fire/minion) DOES NOT benefit from mod such as <span class="text-color -mod">+1 to Level of all # (e.g. Fire/Minion) Skill Gems</span>, since support [skill] gems is not a [active] skill gem.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Lastly, the "base" Support Skill Gems and <a href="/wiki/Awakened_support_gems" class="mw-redirect" title="Awakened support gems">Awakened support gems</a> are considered the same gem. If socketing Awakened and non-Awakened gems together, only the Awakened gem has effects. This also applies to supporting the active skill with two copies of the same Support Skill Gems. In that case, only the higher level Support Skill Gem has effects.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Exceptional_Support_Gems">Exceptional Support Gems</span></h2>
<p>The keyword "Exceptional Support Gems" found on some items refer to the following drop-only gems<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>:
</p>
<ul><li><span class="c-item-hoverbox"><span class="c-item-hoverbox&#95;_activator"><img alt="" src="/w/images/thumb/7/78/Enhance_Support_inventory_icon.png/16px-Enhance_Support_inventory_icon.png" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="16" height="16" srcset="/w/images/thumb/7/78/Enhance_Support_inventory_icon.png/24px-Enhance_Support_inventory_icon.png 1.5x, /w/images/thumb/7/78/Enhance_Support_inventory_icon.png/32px-Enhance_Support_inventory_icon.png 2x" data-file-width="78" data-file-height="78" /><a href="/wiki/Enhance_Support" title="Enhance Support">Enhance Support</a></span><span class="c-item-hoverbox&#95;_display"><span class="item-box -gem"><span class="header -single"><span class="symbol"></span>Enhance Support<span class="symbol"></span></span><span class="item-stats"><span class="group"><a href="/wiki/Category:Exceptional_(gem_tag)" title="Category:Exceptional (gem tag)">Exceptional</a>, <a href="/wiki/Category:Support_(gem_tag)" title="Category:Support (gem tag)">Support</a><br />Icon: <em class="tc -value"><span class="support-gem-id-green">+</span></em><br />Level: <em class="tc -value">(1-3)</em><br />Cost &amp; Reservation Multiplier: <em class="tc -value">120%</em></span><span class="group tc -gemdesc">Supports any skill gem. Once this gem reaches level 2 or above, will raise the quality of supported gems. Cannot support skills that don't come from gems.</span><span class="group tc -mod"><span class="quality"><span class="quality-header"><span><em class="tc -default">Per 1% Quality:</em></span><span class="quality-section-select quality-1 quality-selected">1<span>Superior</span></span><span class="quality-section-select quality-2">2<span>Anomalous</span></span></span><span class="quality-box quality-1 quality-selected">This Gem gains 5% increased Experience</span><span class="quality-box quality-2">3% reduced Dexterity Requirement</span></span></span><span class="group tc -mod">+(0-16)% to Quality of Supported Active Skill Gems</span><span class="group tc -help">This is a Support Gem. It does not grant a bonus to your character, but to skills in sockets connected to it. Place into an item socket connected to a socket containing the Active Skill Gem you wish to augment. <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Version_history">Version history</span></h2>
<table class="wikitable responsive-table">
<tbody><tr>
<th width="10%">Version
</th>
<th>Changes
</th></tr>
<tr>
<td align="center"><a href="/wiki/Version_2.3.0" title="Version 2.3.0">2.3.0</a></td>
<td>
<ul><li>All Support Gems now have Support as part of their name.</li>
<li>When you hover over a socketed Support Gem, it now shows what Skill Gems it affects by making them glow. The same is true for Skill Gems showing what Support Gems affect them. This currently does not properly handle the case of Support Gems that change a Skill Gem so that it enables or disables other Support Gems.</li></ul>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td align="center"><a href="/wiki/Version_0.6.7" title="Version 0.6.7">0.6.7</a></td>
<td>
<ul><li>Introduced to the game. The first gem was <span class="c-item-hoverbox"><span class="c-item-hoverbox&#95;_activator"><img alt="" src="/w/images/thumb/d/d2/Greater_Multiple_Projectiles_Support_inventory_icon.png/16px-Greater_Multiple_Projectiles_Support_inventory_icon.png" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="16" height="16" srcset="/w/images/thumb/d/d2/Greater_Multiple_Projectiles_Support_inventory_icon.png/24px-Greater_Multiple_Projectiles_Support_inventory_icon.png 1.5x, /w/images/thumb/d/d2/Greater_Multiple_Projectiles_Support_inventory_icon.png/32px-Greater_Multiple_Projectiles_Support_inventory_icon.png 2x" data-file-width="78" data-file-height="78" /><a href="/wiki/Greater_Multiple_Projectiles_Support" title="Greater Multiple Projectiles Support">Multiple Projectiles Support</a></span><span class="c-item-hoverbox&#95;_display"><span class="item-box -gem"><span class="header -single"><span class="symbol"></span>Greater Multiple Projectiles Support<span class="symbol"></span></span><span class="item-stats"><span class="group"><a href="/wiki/Category:Support_(gem_tag)" title="Category:Support (gem tag)">Support</a>, <a href="/wiki/Category:Projectile_(gem_tag)" title="Category:Projectile (gem tag)">Projectile</a><br />Icon: <em class="tc -value"><span class="support-gem-id-green">P</span></em><br />Level: <em class="tc -value">(1-20)</em><br />Cost &amp; Reservation Multiplier: <em class="tc -value">150%</em></span><span class="group">Requires Level <em class="tc -value"><em class="tc -value">38</em></em></span><span class="group tc -gemdesc">Supports projectile skills.</span><span class="group tc -mod"><span class="quality"><span class="quality-header"><span><em class="tc -default">Per 1% Quality:</em></span><span class="quality-section-select quality-1 quality-selected">1<span>Superior</span></span><span class="quality-section-select quality-2">2<span>Anomalous</span></span><span class="quality-section-select quality-3">3<span>Divergent</span></span></span><span class="quality-box quality-1 quality-selected">Supported Skills deal 0.5% increased Projectile Damage</span><span class="quality-box quality-2">Supported Skills have 1% reduced Mana Cost<br />Supported Skills have 1% reduced Life Cost<br />Supported Skills have 0.5% increased Projectile Speed</span><span class="quality-box quality-3">Projectiles Fired by Supported Skills have 1% increased Projectile spread</span></span></span><span class="group tc -mod">Supported Skills fire 4 additional Projectiles<br />Supported Skills deal (35-26)% less Projectile Damage</span><span class="group tc -help">This is a Support Gem. It does not grant a bonus to your character, but to skills in sockets connected to it. Place into an item socket connected to a socket containing the Active Skill Gem you wish to augment. Right click to remove from a socket.</span></span></span><img alt="" src="/w/images/d/d2/Greater_Multiple_Projectiles_Support_inventory_icon.png" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="78" height="78" data-file-width="78" data-file-height="78" /></span></span>.</li></ul>
